    <a title="Paula M" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23287093-paula-m"><img alt="Paula M" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1601006204p2/23287093.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1108654159?book_show_action=true">Nov 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Paula M" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Paula M" href="/user/show/23287093-paula-m">Paula M</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23287093-paula-m?shelf=for-review">for-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23287093-paula-m?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1108654159" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4449800156695183380">Maybe because I was never a fan of Romeo and Juliet? Nah. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416415448ra/11959323.gif' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/> <br/><br/>Ethan is oh-so-perfect you guys. Even his foot is <em>yummy.</em><br/><blockquote>
  
    <b>"For a few seconds, I just stare. His foot is beautiful. Perfect. He could be a goddamn foot model." - Cassie.</b>
    <br/>
    <br/>
  
</blockquote><br/><a href='http://herbookthoughts.reads-it.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/tumblr_mpvveva5EY1r33r0fo1_500.gif' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416412825ra/11958049.gif' alt='tumblr_mpvveva5EY1r33r0fo1_500' width='500' height='378' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>And Cassie is virgin and *gasps* nobody can believe it because HELLLOOO PEOPLE, SHE IS SO PRETTTEH AND PURRFECT.<br/><br/><a href='http://herbookthoughts.reads-it.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/tumblr_lni73bAbyK1qj1kpl.gif' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416412825ra/11958050.gif' alt='tumblr_lni73bAbyK1qj1kpl' width='375' height='187' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I want to like this. I really do. But here's the problem: <strong>I don't buy it. Any of it.</strong> The romance, the characters.. everything just fe</span>
  <span id="freeText4449800156695183380" style="display:none">Maybe because I was never a fan of Romeo and Juliet? Nah. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416415448ra/11959323.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <br><br>Ethan is oh-so-perfect you guys. Even his foot is <em>yummy.</em><br><blockquote>
  
    <b>"For a few seconds, I just stare. His foot is beautiful. Perfect. He could be a goddamn foot model." - Cassie.</b>
    <br>
    <br>
  
</blockquote><br><a href="http://herbookthoughts.reads-it.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/tumblr_mpvveva5EY1r33r0fo1_500.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416412825ra/11958049.gif" alt="tumblr_mpvveva5EY1r33r0fo1_500" width="500" height="378" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And Cassie is virgin and *gasps* nobody can believe it because HELLLOOO PEOPLE, SHE IS SO PRETTTEH AND PURRFECT.<br><br><a href="http://herbookthoughts.reads-it.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/tumblr_lni73bAbyK1qj1kpl.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416412825ra/11958050.gif" alt="tumblr_lni73bAbyK1qj1kpl" width="375" height="187" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I want to like this. I really do. But here's the problem: <strong>I don't buy it. Any of it.</strong> The romance, the characters.. everything just feels so forced. They can have sex every day or have that ~very hot connection~ between them, I still don't buy it. I don't even care about that <em>CHEMISTRY</em> that everybody is speaking of. <strong>EXCUSE ME BUT WHERE? WHERE IS THE LOVE STORY THAT YOU PROMISED?</strong> This book made Bella and Edward's ~love story~ more interesting.<br><br>Ethan Holt was heartbroken so he doesn't date. He's having a hard time committing to a relationship. Whatever. He has issues. Baggage. But Cassie doesn't care about that because she's a virgin and Ethan is making her feel things so she wants him to deflower her. Oh but perfect Ethan have hurty feelings and he thinks Cassie 'deserves better' so he tries to stay away and just be an asshat. But Cassie is a martyr!!! <strong>She doesn't care even if he's being a douche and that the guy is unhinge because they have ~connection~ and CHEMISTRY.</strong> SHE wants HIM. And that my friends is how the girl became obsess. <br><br>And that's what the book is just about. <strong>A virgin girl. A destructive boy. An unhealthy relationship. And chapters with them just lusting at each other.</strong> Seriously, why did I even. I should have just listened to the mess in our house and gave my attention to them.<br><br>Every time I turn a chapter, I keep hoping that the plot will eventually turn around and be about Cassie's self realizations. Because at the first few chapters that's what the book is about. It's supposed to be about Cassie finding herself because she have no idea who she is. And acting is her passion. Oh and also thinking erotic thoughts about Ethan Holt.<br><br>BUT THIS IS WHY I DIDN'T REALLY LIKE THIS: I actually expected this, I mean, this is NA. But I also expected it to have a heart. To have a meaning. That even though some chapters are just them lusting each other, I will say "YES, THEY BELONG TO EACH AND THEIR LOVE IS REAL" But no, this is the most BS of all the BS book relationship I've read. <strong>AND THIS GIRL HAVE NO SELF RESPECT.</strong> I have a lot of Virgin friends and yes, they feel lonely. And yes, they think about sex but they're not like Cassie who thinks and writes about a guy's peen in her diary because she's fascinated. <br><br>Cassie says thing like this:<br><blockquote>
  "No, I didn't know it was a fluffing porn term. Do I look like a porn-watching pervert.."
</blockquote><br>And then watches porn after. <br><br><a href="http://herbookthoughts.reads-it.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/Do_I_need_to_slap_you_with_a_p.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416412825ra/11958051.gif" alt="Do_I_need_to_slap_you_with_a_p" width="250" height="176" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The guys a pig. 'Nuff said. Seriously, who falls in love with a guy like this?! <br><br>The writing is decent that's why I added a star rating. And that's the only good thing I can say. I<br><br>(I might add more to this review but this whole thing is typed right after I finished the book. Yes, I finished it. Pat in the back for me.)<br><br>You can also read my review <a href="http://herbookthoughts.reads-it.com/?p=1898" rel="nofollow noopener">HERE.</a></span>

<div id="review_1204738594" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1204738594" />
    <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously"><img alt="Rachel Reads Ravenously" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1539149211p2/14514998.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1204738594?book_show_action=true">Feb 18, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel Reads Ravenously" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously">Rachel Reads Ravenously</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781250063274" href="/book/show/22213598-bad-romeo">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=library-checkout">library-checkout</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=new-adult-mania">new-adult-mania</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=angsty-intense">angsty-intense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=guilty-pleasure-read">guilty-pleasure-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=men-can-be-stupid-sometimes">men-can-be-stupid-sometimes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=college-romance">college-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1204738594" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5040783246446440176"><b> 4.5 stars! </b><br/><br/><b> <i> “Sometimes people put up walls, not only to keep people out, but also to see who cares enough to tear them down.” </i> </b><br/><br/><a href='http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/badromeo.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424316649i/13745423.png' alt=' photo badromeo.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>So, guess who loved this book when most everyone else didn't?<br/><br/><a href='http://reactiongifs.com/?p=3944' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394920213ra/8924631.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Guilty as charged. To be fair, I am a total angst whore and gobbled this book up. Want to know what's even scarier? For all of the angst this book doles out, I've read angstier!<br/><br/>This is the story of Cassie and Ethan, who met when they were young aspiring actors. The book begins in the present, three ye</span>
  <span id="freeText5040783246446440176" style="display:none"><b> 4.5 stars! </b><br><br><b> <i> “Sometimes people put up walls, not only to keep people out, but also to see who cares enough to tear them down.” </i> </b><br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/badromeo.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424316649i/13745423.png" alt=" photo badromeo.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So, guess who loved this book when most everyone else didn't?<br><br><a href="http://reactiongifs.com/?p=3944" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394920213ra/8924631.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Guilty as charged. To be fair, I am a total angst whore and gobbled this book up. Want to know what's even scarier? For all of the angst this book doles out, I've read angstier!<br><br>This is the story of Cassie and Ethan, who met when they were young aspiring actors. The book begins in the present, three years after Ethan shattered Cassie's heart, and the two of them are cast as the leads in a new Broadway play. Ethan, after all of the shit he put Cassie through, is desperate to get her back but Cassie won't let him back in easy.<br><br>This book alternates between the present and the past, giving the reader both sides of Cassie and Ethan. Cassie who in the past was a horny, naive virgin and in the present a jaded and bitter woman. Ethan, a dark storm cloud in the past more closed up than a tight clam shell, and in the present a man who had worked through his issues and wants to be redeemed.<br><br>I think one of the reasons I enjoyed this book so much was because I went into it with the absolute lowest expectations. I also read the spoilers ahead of time and knew the ending would be a cliffhanger and many questions would not be answered, so I came into this book prepared. So many people hated or disliked this book, but I still gave it a shot because my local library has a copy. And if it's free, why not? Well, I'm glad I did. For me, this book was unputdownable. <br><br>I will say I did not care for the whiplash, but in order for a guy to redeem himself, he has to be a dick right? Yeah, Ethan was a dick. But, I felt like he really did change by the time he was an adult. I just really wish I knew what horrible thing he did to Cassie BECAUSE THE AUTHOR DIDN'T TELL US IN THIS BOOK!!!<br><br>And the other thing I didn't care for? That vagina slow clapping line. My god I cringed when I read that. I think it was supposed to be funny, but this was me reading it instead:<br><a href="http://reactiongifs.com/?p=23616" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424316649ra/13745424.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Anywoo, if you like angst and men trying to make up for their colossal mistakes, this book is the one for you! I'm actually really excited for book 2 and some answers.<br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="5040783246446440176" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

They are complicated and real, and I was completely wrapped up in their journey.<br><br><i>
  <b>"I warned you," he says, breathing heavily and cupping my face. "Why the hell didn't you listen?"</b>
</i><br><br>When Ethan and Cassie first cross paths, she is young, and naive with big dreams, while he is jaded, pessimistic and determined not to let anyone in. But when they are cast opposite each other in one of histories most tragically, beautiful love stories, they find themselves unable to resist their intense connection. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420341222i/13206924._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now three years later with tons of regret and heartache, Ethan and Cassie find themselves thrown together once again, will Ethan be able to gain Cassie's forgiveness, or are these two doomed to fail all over again?<br><br><i>
  <b>"Nothing was enough for me after you."</b>
</i><br><br><i>Bad Romeo</i> was a well-crafted, realistic love story, filled with humor, intense characters and scorching hot sexual tension. While this story may not be for some, I really enjoyed it. <div id="review_1534620582" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1534620582" />
    <a title="Beverly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly"><img alt="Beverly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466964369p2/13095060.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1534620582?book_show_action=true">Feb 02, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beverly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beverly" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly">Beverly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1534620582" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5724367675262204870">I went into this story pretty much blind. I just remember a lot of my friends read and loved this book last year. So when the story began I wasn’t expecting how much I would love it. First, the story is awesome, but I am absolutely in love with how the story is told. Cassie and Ethan were college lovers, sweethearts, I don’t know what to call them, there isn’t really an adequate term for them. Regardless, they dated in college and while you don’t know all the details when you get started you kno</span>
  <span id="freeText5724367675262204870" style="display:none">I went into this story pretty much blind. I just remember a lot of my friends read and loved this book last year. So when the story began I wasn’t expecting how much I would love it. First, the story is awesome, but I am absolutely in love with how the story is told. Cassie and Ethan were college lovers, sweethearts, I don’t know what to call them, there isn’t really an adequate term for them. Regardless, they dated in college and while you don’t know all the details when you get started you know their connection was strong. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454982805i/18037082._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>We learn about Ethan and Cassie’s past by the reflections back. See when the story begins they are both adults and have been cast in a play together. All we know is that they dated and do not get along, at all. I loved seeing where their current emotions came from and the reflections did just that. I felt like we lived that time with them. This way of story telling allowed me to really understand their motives and thoughts. <br><br>Cassie is a people pleaser and has always been what she felt like people wanted. She is unsure of herself and completely lost when she begins drama school. Ethan is the older, knows who he is and doesn’t take anyone’s shit. His first reaction to Cassie is frustration, he see’s this beautiful girl trying to be anyone but herself. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454982805i/18037083._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book is just so much. I loved seeing Cassie come into her own. I loved watching Ethan open up. I loved watching them fall in love. I loved the other characters, they added so much humor. Like I already said, I love the way it was told. This isn’t my favorite type of story telling, but I can’t imagine this story being any other way. It allowed my emotions, thoughts and feels to just go back and forth.<br><br>I can’t believe I waited so long to read this fantastic book and I cannot recommend it enough, absolutely love it! The good thing about waiting, I can jump right into <i>Broken Juliet.</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454982805i/18037084._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>I am listening to the audiobook. </i><br><br><i>Teasers created by me with stock images purchased from depositphotos.</i><br><br>
  <a href="http://readingissexybookblog.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423003910i/13574955.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
<br>
  <a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/Reading-is-Sexy-Book-Blog/717861984979600" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <span id="freeText18140666917638523498" style="display:none"><i>Attention all the -Bad Romeo- lovers!!! <br>Bad Romeo is going to be a short movie. I'm soooooo freaking excited for this! Yaaaaay! :D </i><br><br>Full trailer is finally out! ☺☺☺<br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://youtu.be/RBcySdfmB-8">https://youtu.be/RBcySdfmB-8</a><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1463999826ra/19182965.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>-----------------------------<br><br><b>My book review:</b><br>First of all I'm mentally slapping my face cause God sometimes I'm acting really stupid. Why the hell I wait for months to read this mind blowing book? All this time why the fuck I wait to meet Mr.Ethan Holt? Dear God, I'm begging you. Pls forbid me to do this kind of stupid decision in the near future. I'm counting on you. Thank you &amp; Amen!:)<br><br>Ok let's back to Mr.Holt! Yeah, that mind fucking, sexy, funny, cool, cute but broken boy. He's an asshole for breaking Cassie's precious heart that's for sure BUT yeah, always comes a BUT I'm totally understand him. Cause in the past I was so scared to say "I love you" to someone... Of course his reasons different from mine but still I really, really understand him why he's so scare to say those words.. Anyway he made a mistake, I know it's fair to swear him, scream him or judge him by his actions but you're so wrong. He's a broken, damaged boy. Not physically damaged but he's feeling emotionally insecure. <br><br>Because--&gt; <b>
  <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ (When he was 16 years old he learned that he's adopted and he scared to attached someone because he thinks if he do that no matter what he do, no matter how much he love them won't work out cause he thinks still people will leave him just like his real parents. So he's afraid to open himself to someone and also fall in love with Cassie too. ) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>
</b><br><br>When you read the book I'm sure first you won't like him but after you finish the book. God, when you finish this amazing book you'll understand him and you'll fall in love him much more... Cause he knows his fault, he knows what he fucked up in the past and now he's back to earn her heart again and he's really pushing Cassie to forgive him and he's really trying to things work out and I believe him with all my heart... Maybe it's not easy to forgive someone who broke your heart but everybody deserves 2nd chance right? I hope Cassie gives him this chance. :)<br><br>What can I say more? This story, this book will give you a lot of laughter, a lot of swooning moments. Ethan &amp; Cassie's chemistry were so amazing, I felt like they were real but especially their first kiss and first making love scenes are so beautiful, so precious... I'll never forget those scenes. :) I really recommend this book to everyone and pls do yourself a favor and give this book a chance... Cause you know Ethan deserves it too. Don't break his heart.Please! :)<br><br>This is exactly me while I read this book!!! :)<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1460988038ra/18809833.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445178364ra/16611499.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1399279299ra/9529057.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1432174432ra/14907190.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>---------------------------<br><br><b>Attention all the -Bad Romeo- lovers!!! <br><br>Bad Romeo is going to be a short movie. I'm soooooo freaking excited for this! <span id="freeTextContainer1650002517683908710">It was really nice writing for a debut novel, <b>but this book was like boobs without nipples, POINTLESS.</b><br/>I don't see what happened here!? What was the big issue? I didn't feel the frustration I'm guessing I should have felt for Cassie, I didn't feel sad for Ethan.<br/>It didn't really bring about feeling inside of me.<br/><br/><i>*may contain veryyyy little blips of spoilers*</i><br/><br/>I will read the second book, because the author has a nice way of writing, it was compelling, but it is the story I have a problem with. I mean</span>
  <span id="freeText1650002517683908710" style="display:none">It was really nice writing for a debut novel, <b>but this book was like boobs without nipples, POINTLESS.</b><br />I don't see what happened here!? What was the big issue? I didn't feel the frustration I'm guessing I should have felt for Cassie, I didn't feel sad for Ethan.<br />It didn't really bring about feeling inside of me.<br /><br /><i>*may contain veryyyy little blips of spoilers*</i><br /><br />I will read the second book, because the author has a nice way of writing, it was compelling, but it is the story I have a problem with. I mean, why? Whats the whole point? Ending it that way, with nothing much 'OMG' happening in this book. Pretty pissing off. I was waiting for the drama, explosion of emotions.. I got NADA. Its a second chance love story, I'm a sucker for those because they make me all 'AWWWWWW' and I'm always abusing the chick to take the stupid knuckle-headed guy back, but here IDK what was even happening for me to feel anything much or root for anyone because I DO NOT KNOW WHAT HAS HAPPENED BETWEEN THE TWO OF THEM. o.O<br /><br />All I know is, they are theater students, now theater actors, the guy had a littttttle baggage, she was HORNY like 24x7 and they had crazy chemistry and now she's jaded. I saw nothing happening here. I'm pissed, because it was a looooooong book with no base to keep stuff running; at least it seamed that way in this book, I'll keep an eye out for book two and see where this goes, because it ended without much being revealed.<br /><br />I thought they were generally bipolar, because of their weird mood swings, he was manipulating without even trying and she had no backbone. </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=second-chance">second-chance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=cotton-candy-romance">cotton-candy-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=oh-the-angst">oh-the-angst</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1103812740" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8566956714283590762"><b>4 Romeo Stars. </b>	<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417470919i/12389957.jpg' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Cassie heart was broken one time, and she never recovered from it completely. But when the cause of your broken heart is far away, coping is easier. But what happens when he suddenly is next working next to you, having to see him every day?<br/>Life throws Cassie and Ethan together one more time, as the lead actors of Romeo and Juliet. (How ironic, right?) Ethan knows he broke Cassie’s heart in acting school but he was a broken man himself and thought he was doing the best, but now, a</span>
  <span id="freeText8566956714283590762" style="display:none"><b>4 Romeo Stars. </b>	<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417470919i/12389957.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Cassie heart was broken one time, and she never recovered from it completely. But when the cause of your broken heart is far away, coping is easier. But what happens when he suddenly is next working next to you, having to see him every day?<br>Life throws Cassie and Ethan together one more time, as the lead actors of Romeo and Juliet. (How ironic, right?) Ethan knows he broke Cassie’s heart in acting school but he was a broken man himself and thought he was doing the best, but now, a few years later he regrets it and want her back. And he makes that pretty clear. <br>But Cassie knows the pain of a broken heart. Will she risk breaking it one more time? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1417470919ra/12389958.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Let me be really honest in this one (well, that’s kind of the point…): I really liked the plot, I like how he was delivered and the writing was good with a nice flow. This book has a lot of potential and I do believe that for a debut novel the story was pleasingly delivered. I just had some minor “twitches” with it. First was the characters (see below), second, despite liking the “back and forth” during the chapters, that allowed to see their past and what happened before between them, sometimes it changed abruptly making it difficult for readers to fully connect with the progression of the story. And last but not least: the “now I love you. Now I don’t” thing, not only created unnecessary angst but also made the story run in circles turning it slightly repetitive. <br>But in the end of the day, this was a great debut and emotional reading and I can’t wait to rad what will happen next. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402872274i/10002999.jpg" width="350" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>Rating: </b> 4 Stars. <br> <b>Characters Development: </b> Cassie was annoying with her stubbornness, sometimes unjustified. But since she was broken once, we could understand her actions until a certain point. She was not my favorite heroine so far, but she was nice enough. Ethan was good when he was being honest and sweet. But in the moments he changed his mind and turned into an asshole I just wanted to beat him. I love the relationship between those two, they were great together… and not only when they were acting. <br> <b>Steam: </b> Hot moments. Not to mention Cassie is horny as a bunny. <br> <b>Sensible Subjects: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Not really. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <b>Love Triangle: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <b>HEA: </b>	<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Mild Cliffhanger. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br> <i>*ARC kindly provided in exchange of honest review.*</i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1875056178" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11801881808014282726">This book was such an emotional rollercoaster! I laughed, cried, raged (because OW and OM, seriously authors stop doing that!!!) swoon (repeatedly) and overall enjoyed myself. I'm so reading the sequel but I can't give this book 5 stars because it has everything I hate in a book and more! <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ <br/>1) Slutshaming, seriously authors you are women, too. Will you ever stop condeming other women's sexual decisions? It was particularly annoying here because h might be subject of slutshaming in </span></span>
  <span id="freeText11801881808014282726" style="display:none">This book was such an emotional rollercoaster! I laughed, cried, raged (because OW and OM, seriously authors stop doing that!!!) swoon (repeatedly) and overall enjoyed myself. I'm so reading the sequel but I can't give this book 5 stars because it has everything I hate in a book and more! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ <br />1) Slutshaming, seriously authors you are women, too. Will you ever stop condeming other women's sexual decisions? It was particularly annoying here because h might be subject of slutshaming in other books and in real life because she sleeps around a lot! Who does she think she is to call Zoe a slut?<br /><br />2) OW and OM. In real life, I can understand when people sleep around as long as no one gets hurt, but in this story everybody got hurt! This is supposed to be a romance book. I didn't need a full, graphic detail of what happened between h and Paris... I meant Connor. The romance was ruined for me, but there was something about the writing that kept me reading. <br /><br />3) Heroine wasn't H's first love, and his reason to act like a douche made me think that this Vanessa girl was more important to him than Cassie at that moment. Cassie was supposed to be the love of his life so all this mentioning of OW are so off-putting. This isn't a safe read. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />It might seem that I hated the book, but I didn't. In fact, Ethan is already one of my book boyfriends, (provisionally, I hope book 2 doesn't ruin him) but I won't fancast him like I do in some of my reviews. Not until I finish book 2 and until I find a gif. I need a gif for this book. Not of the hero but of the reaction he brings on Cassie.<br /><br />Does anyone have a slow-clapping-vagina gif??? LOL I'll need it for my review! Cassie's train of thought was rather silly that way. <br /><br />I want to write a longer review because Cassie's first time and the things I love about this book deserve more!!! If I had to choose my top 10 defloration scenes in books Cassie's will be certainly one of them. So sweet! I felt like I was there. I also love the sexual chemistry and all the description of their casting, their rehearsals, their acting classes. It was fascinating.<br /><br />I'm on book 2 now. <br /><br />So does anyone have a slow-clapping vagina gif? LOL I'll need one for my longer review.</span>

<div id="review_1110540874" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1110540874" />
    <a title="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts"><img alt="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591195447p2/16496589.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1110540874?book_show_action=true">Nov 19, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" href="/user/show/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts">Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts?shelf=advance-copy">advance-copy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1110540874" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2168969891241728759"><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419966458i/13151116._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/> <br/>It’s about courage, hope, love and a<i>
  <b> Bad Romeo.</b>
</i><br/><br/>I so enjoyed this completely character driven story. The prose is just wonderful, the dialogue perfection. Bad Romeo is stunning in its New Adult articulation and made me <i>
  <b>feel </b>
</i>so much. <b>I didn’t want to put this book down.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421856671i/13422374.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Bad Romeo rolls between present day and six years past to a time when they first met, a time when he fought their connection and she just wanted him to take her....<i> A time when their relationship was a secret....</i> The way th</span>
  <span id="freeText2168969891241728759" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419966458i/13151116._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>It’s about courage, hope, love and a<i>
  <b> Bad Romeo.</b>
</i><br><br>I so enjoyed this completely character driven story. The prose is just wonderful, the dialogue perfection. Bad Romeo is stunning in its New Adult articulation and made me <i>
  <b>feel </b>
</i>so much. <b>I didn’t want to put this book down.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421856671i/13422374.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Bad Romeo rolls between present day and six years past to a time when they first met, a time when he fought their connection and she just wanted him to take her....<i> A time when their relationship was a secret....</i> The way the story dipped in and out of each period worked so well; it always left me wanting more from each era and showed the perfect character development from past to present.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421851024i/13421799.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ethan Holt is the present day darling of the theatre world. He’s completely frustrating at times but also sexy, charismatic, extremely handsome and an expert in his craft..... He’s adored by so many but something happened way back in his past to bring out his arsehole tendencies. <i>He's utterly loveable all the same.</i><br><br>Cassie Taylor is a wannabe theatre actress when we're initially introduced, what I also craved for her was fulfilment in her personal life. I love her inner witty monologue that's laced with self-deprecating humour and her foot-in-mouth syndrome that allows her thoughts to slip out during the most inopportune times, providing delightful comedic value and cringe worthy moments.<br> <br>They both have issues to overcome....<br>The question is can they do this and be together?<br><br><b>It gave me the heart flutter romantic melts…. It's simply beautiful.</b> <br><br>Ethan and Cassie have the most wonderful flirtatious banter, especially when they first meet. The author showed me in glorious pictures the intense chemistry and connection between them, she showed me why they were unable to be apart. Yes, there is what some would consider a little back and forth, especially as we see both the past and present of their relationship, but for me this mattered not, it simply added to the tension and angst of the story. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421856573i/13422360.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The light and shade of the text is captivating, the juxtaposition of their passion and desire to the hilarity of some of the situations they found themselves in is wonderful. Their pure carnal desires for each other and their desperate need shines through in one moment and then in the next the author had me smiling with them in mortification.<br><br><i>The E-mails....</i> they're so beautiful and made my heart hurt.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421856573i/13422361.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I could have taken more of a steam factor and I wish <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the ultimate moment had been sooner  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>but I completely understand why the author went this way with the story. The waiting let us experience their desperation and anticipation, the build-up of their sexual tension and then..... The intensity and depth of emotion was greater, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ the devastation, even more poignant.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br>The ending was an OH. My. Goodness.... But I'm sure this will lead perfectly to book 2 of the series.<b> I highly recommend <b>Bad Romeo</b> to all lovers of New Adult Romance stories with a witty personality.</b> The authenticity of the dialogue and the consistency of it made the story flow so beautifully and this, combined with the ironic and self-deprecating cringe worthy moments, made it simply a delight to experience. <b>Pure loveliness</b><br><br><br>Complimentary copy received from the publishers, via NetGalley, in exchange for an honest review.<br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

Now that they are back together for an acting role, Ethan wants to make up for being a complete tosser and is trying to win Cassie back.<br/><br/>We didn't get any answers whatsoever, very frustrating. I didn't find it angsty, just extremely annoying. Ethan was a dick, and Cassie was a bit of a doormat.<br/><br/>Still, I signed up for book 2 already </span>

I didn't find it angsty, just extremely annoying. Ethan was a dick, and Cassie was a bit of a doormat.<br /><br />Still, I signed up for book 2 already so I HOPE it's worth it.</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1980612851?book_show_action=true">Apr 24, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nissa | Of Pens and Pages Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nissa | Of Pens and Pages Book Blog" href="/user/show/41356020-nissa-of-pens-and-pages-book-blog">Nissa | Of Pens and Pages Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41356020-nissa-of-pens-and-pages-book-blog?shelf=female-pov">female-pov</a>,

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1980612851" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2854219748340504325"><b> 2 stars</b><br/><br/><a href='http://ofpensandpages.com' rel='nofollow noopener'>Reviews and more at Of Pens and Pages.</a><br/><br/><b>I'm joining the minority on this one.</b> I really wanted to like this book, but it fell flat for me. I wanted to smack the main characters so hard, my palm was actually itching to do it.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1440522642ra/15986864.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Second chance romances are usually filled with angst, but also love and hope. I suppose <i>Bad Romeo</i> had those, too. <b>The premise was interesting and was what I usually love.</b> Former lovers reunite to work together. Bonus points for being actors and being paired up as lovers </span>
  <span id="freeText2854219748340504325" style="display:none"><b> 2 stars</b><br><br><a href="http://ofpensandpages.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Reviews and more at Of Pens and Pages.</a><br><br><b>I'm joining the minority on this one.</b> I really wanted to like this book, but it fell flat for me. I wanted to smack the main characters so hard, my palm was actually itching to do it.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1440522642ra/15986864.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Second chance romances are usually filled with angst, but also love and hope. I suppose <i>Bad Romeo</i> had those, too. <b>The premise was interesting and was what I usually love.</b> Former lovers reunite to work together. Bonus points for being actors and being paired up as lovers in the production. The hero wants to win back the heroine, but their past scarred the heroine too much.<br><br>Despite the lovely premise, a lot of things in the book frustrated me.<br><br><b>I disliked both leads.</b> Ethan was a douchebag who kept on stringing along Cassie, and Cassie was a doormat who was led on by her libido. She knows she doesn't deserve what he's doing, but a kiss and some groping action, and she's panting over him again. Toss the dog a bone, yada, yada, yada. I couldn't find it in me to feel bad for her.<br><br>Even after three years since their break up, <b>I didn't see character growth.</b> It was frustrating. I'm so frustrated!<br><br><b>The story became repetitive fast.</b> A lot of "we shouldn't, but oh god, we can't stop" going on. The pacing became too slow for my taste because the same thing kept happening between these two. Cue urge to maim someone again. If we cut the repetitive crap happening in the past, maybe this duet could fit in one book. I should have worn a protective suit because <b>their relationship is toxic.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1493021767ra/22575821.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And after going in unnecessary circles, <b>we still don't find out what happened between the two.</b> As much as I want to drop this story, I can't <b>not</b> know what happened. But ugh if we could just get on in the present and see what happens, that would be great.<br><br>Fortunately, the sequel has long been out, and I'm still not giving up. Despite my frustrations, I really enjoyed the author's writing style, and I liked Mister Romance, her upcoming book.<br><br><i>Bad Romeo</i> is the first book in the Starcrossed series and is <b>told in Cassie's POV</b>. The story alternates between the past and the present and ends with a cliffhanger.<br><br><a href="http://ofpensandpages.com" rel="nofollow noopener"> Blog</a> | <a href="http://facebook.com/ofpensandpages" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> | <a href="http://twitter.com/ofpensandpages" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://instagram.com/nissareads" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1081990759?book_show_action=true">Oct 16, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pavlina Read more sleep less blog❤❤  " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pavlina Read more sleep less blog❤❤  " href="/user/show/6603203-pavlina-read-more-sleep-less-blog">Pavlina Read more sleep less blog❤❤  </a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6603203-pavlina-read-more-sleep-less-blog?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1081990759" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2626106116975273184">3 STARS<br/><br/>I had read so many reviews about this one and most of them were 4-5 stars so I had high expectations when I start reading it! In the beginning I was intrigued and very interested to see what would happen but after 30% I started rolling my eyes so many times and feeling so frustrated with the sexual tension and their acts which make me lose interest for the story and the characters!<br/>Another problem I had was the switching between the present and the past and sometimes I would forget where I</span>
  <span id="freeText2626106116975273184" style="display:none">3 STARS<br><br>I had read so many reviews about this one and most of them were 4-5 stars so I had high expectations when I start reading it! In the beginning I was intrigued and very interested to see what would happen but after 30% I started rolling my eyes so many times and feeling so frustrated with the sexual tension and their acts which make me lose interest for the story and the characters!<br>Another problem I had was the switching between the present and the past and sometimes I would forget where I was.. In my opinion it would be better if there wasn't the past. I don't think it was necessary. Apart from this, I didn't like the characters a lot! Holt didn't win me over at all! He annoyed me so many times. And Cassie...oh Cassie you are totally stupid for me!<br>My conclusion for this book? This book will either be a hit or miss for readers. I'm in the middle because there are moments I liked it and moments I didn't like it at all! Would I consider reading the second book? Well yes because I want to see what will happen even though I'm not a fan of the characters! Hopefully the second book will be much better!<br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426249906i/13992592.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>ARC provided by St. Martin's Press via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review</span>
  <a data-text-id="2626106116975273184" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katy Loves Romance ❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katy Loves Romance ❤️" href="/user/show/10247668-katy-loves-romance">Katy Loves Romance ❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10247668-katy-loves-romance?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10247668-katy-loves-romance?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>,

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1121359113" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer951370939922631819"> <a href='http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/B115180D-F083-42F6-A7BB-AD390BBBABB6_zpsrfcbxaqy.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423599925i/13649118._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo B115180D-F083-42F6-A7BB-AD390BBBABB6_zpsrfcbxaqy.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/> <br/>I have been umming and arring on how to star this book because I have so many feelings on certain aspects of the story I loved it but then things got a little much too so for that reason I'm going to review it in two half's and do it slightly differently. First and foremost this was an intense, passionate and gripping book for me yet I expected certain parts to unfold quicker so let me explain. <br/> <br/><b>First Half 5 Stars*****</b><br/>You begin where Cassie is enisted to take part in a new role on a perfor</span>
  <span id="freeText951370939922631819" style="display:none"> <a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/B115180D-F083-42F6-A7BB-AD390BBBABB6_zpsrfcbxaqy.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423599925i/13649118._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo B115180D-F083-42F6-A7BB-AD390BBBABB6_zpsrfcbxaqy.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>I have been umming and arring on how to star this book because I have so many feelings on certain aspects of the story I loved it but then things got a little much too so for that reason I'm going to review it in two half's and do it slightly differently. First and foremost this was an intense, passionate and gripping book for me yet I expected certain parts to unfold quicker so let me explain. <br> <br><b>First Half 5 Stars*****</b><br>You begin where Cassie is enisted to take part in a new role on a performance, she's an actress her job is working in the arts and it's something she exceeds at, she loves it. What I loved was the ability the writer gave me was that I had the feelings of being part of the audience and watching the performance with my own eyes just like reading, I got the tingles and feels a sense of enforeyer as such when you are at the theatre and a big part of the story had me at grips with the feels in that way. <br> <br>Ethan asked to be part of the role right alongside Cassie he didn't know what it was but he <b>NEEDED</b> to be there with her. <b>This is in present day.</b><br> <br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/9DAAF784-5C08-4017-BDF3-A0EFCE366D85_zpstd26w0a7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423599925i/13649119._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 9DAAF784-5C08-4017-BDF3-A0EFCE366D85_zpstd26w0a7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>It begins in present day then flits back and forth to six years ago when Ethan struggled with his feelings and what he should or should not feel, where they met when they are both auditioning to get into the best drama and arts school and where they have to work together to get in and in to doing so they have to perform together this gives them a start of a friendship where they keep bumping into each other and once they move forward in their new lives and start college they become connected to each other where they want each other and have instant chemistry that pulled at my heart (not that Ethan wanted it that way but it was that way) I could see at the beginning how much they had a sense of comfort in each other, they became entwined in each others lives and emotionally this was a very much character driven book. <br><br> <br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/EC1DFF04-5186-4F17-B534-EA9E00C44E76_zpsvurbmal3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423599925i/13649120._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo EC1DFF04-5186-4F17-B534-EA9E00C44E76_zpsvurbmal3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br> <br>On stage they have this Intense chemistry that all that are involved and all that are watching are gripped and watching, feeling there movements, there initial movements, there touches, kisses I was mesmerised at this point of the story and was so excited to see how their chemistry would be on stage and <b>OFF</b>. But off stage Ethan has a lot of demons and in that he is unable to do what Cassie wants and let himself feel what you as a reader can feel I mean theres no doubt about that from get go. <br><br> <br><br><b>Let me explain a little about Cassie</b>; Cassie is innocent and hasn't had a boyfriend before nor anyone she has been attracted to the way she does Ethan, therefore I had myself laughing at her thoughts how she was quite childlike at times I mean she just said things she felt with no qualms about it <b>I want to suck your penis etc?</b> Very innocent behaviour she so funny yet there was an after embarrassment that I wanted to hug her and lead her to how she should behave yet Ethan was good with her here but then he walked away then came back again and in that mixed communication occurred and self doubt creeped in. <br><br> <br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/7D39247D-094B-4C09-9BA4-4BD9554D295A_zps0mtdk48y.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423599925i/13649121._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 7D39247D-094B-4C09-9BA4-4BD9554D295A_zps0mtdk48y.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br> <br>Yet in present day he does nothing but show himself fully and how he wants to start over, how he wants to be all that she needs and not let his past demons interfere with how much he wants to move forward in a much maturer way. Above all in the first half I adored how it held onto my heart, captivated me I was completely engrossed by <b>THEM</b>. <br><br> <br><b>Second half 3 Stars***</b><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/4D1642C8-DCA3-456B-AF7D-4C72E4676D3B_zpsvxjgszlt.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423599925i/13649122._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 4D1642C8-DCA3-456B-AF7D-4C72E4676D3B_zpsvxjgszlt.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br> <br>I love angst I love the feel of will they won't they I love the feelings I get when I read these kind of love stories and I am first in line when I read those kind of blurbs which is why I went and read this one, I mean I actually liked and loved the only rock go there is in Kellen Kyle and I wasn't that upset with Kiera ccause all in all I knew who she was meant to be with at the end what I'm saying is when I see a goal in sight I'm all in, but here the word <b>BAD ROMEO</b> had a hugeee factor in this story. So my status updates 40% and you are dealing with Dry humping where the flirtish banter was fun that it didn't really worry me at that point but then we get to 50% and we're still there is the same point, then status update at 70%....... <br><br><b>
  <blockquote> For the love of god will these two stop the dry humping and just take THE DAMN CLOTHES OFF THE GET IT ON!!!!!! </blockquote>
</b> <br><blockquote>
  <a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/gifs/sexual%20frustraion%20gif_zpsvksmiuju.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420037431ra/13157519.gif" alt=" photo sexual frustraion gif_zpsvksmiuju.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</blockquote><br> <br>It got a little thin and I was wondering where it was headed???!!! I love damaged heros I love broken men and there inner turmoil that doesn't bother me at all but there has to be a part of you that clicks and decides to take a chance. <br><br>Saying all that I did enjoy it, it is a NA but I just felt I could of moved forward faster or cut short a little, but I am most definitely excited for book 2 I want closure and I want them both to be happy. I'm really hoping for more a mature outlook and to see them both connect on a more intimate level and to <b>OPEN UP TO TAKE THAT CHANCE AND NOT CLOSE UP!!!</b> <br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/275B3805-2550-4154-A213-DE458BFFB44E_zpsesjgavv1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423599925i/13649123._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 275B3805-2550-4154-A213-DE458BFFB44E_zpsesjgavv1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>Overall 3.75-4 stars****</b><br><br><b>That is all</b><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/Slut%20Sistas%20Book%20Blog/4C9AABC8-2B5D-4055-97E1-777989BF51A3_zpsifeeusfn.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422477954i/13505287.jpg" alt=" photo 4C9AABC8-2B5D-4055-97E1-777989BF51A3_zpsifeeusfn.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br><br>For more reviews follow us here:<br><a href="http://slutsistas.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_1769151052" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1769151052" />
    <a title="XxTainaxX Curvy and Nerdy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/19719801-xxtainaxx-curvy-and-nerdy"><img alt="XxTainaxX Curvy and Nerdy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1569767603p2/19719801.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1769151052?book_show_action=true">Sep 29, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="XxTainaxX Curvy and Nerdy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="XxTainaxX Curvy and Nerdy" href="/user/show/19719801-xxtainaxx-curvy-and-nerdy">XxTainaxX Curvy and Nerdy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1769151052" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7714863451936773402">Let me start by saying that this story is stocked full with angst. It can get pretty thick sometimes to the point of frustration but if you're patient, you can peel back the layers and come out of the experience with a pretty meaningful love story. Not only in the romantic couple way but in the self love category as well. I had to stop a few times and talk myself into picking it back up thinking "Do I really want to do this to myself?" I'm really glad I kept going. Ethan and Cassie meet in colle</span>
  <span id="freeText7714863451936773402" style="display:none">Let me start by saying that this story is stocked full with angst. It can get pretty thick sometimes to the point of frustration but if you're patient, you can peel back the layers and come out of the experience with a pretty meaningful love story. Not only in the romantic couple way but in the self love category as well. I had to stop a few times and talk myself into picking it back up thinking "Do I really want to do this to myself?" I'm really glad I kept going. Ethan and Cassie meet in college as they are auditioning for admission into a prestigious art school. Despite some pretty heavy resistance on Ethan's part, they start something that flourishes into love pretty quickly. But love isn't so clear cut and easy when you're struggling with your demons. For a while it works, then it doesn't. 8 years after they are last together, the couple has to work together on the stage again. The story goes through what happened in the past while interjecting with them now. The back and forth jump in the timelines can be confusing at times when listening in audiobook. While Ethan was displaying signs he had changed in the present. I found myself as skeptical as Cassie as their past got recounted. I liked that the author was able to evoke that. Ethan was a very troubled character with deep scars that affected him greatly. While his reasons for being that way, to me, seem a fairly common occurrence, I liked that the story shows that it doesn't matter what anyone else thinks or perceives, it's about the person that's feeling it. Cassie started out fine and was later changed by her experiences so the contrast was very interesting. Towards the end of this story I was feeling a little more hopeful about Ethan, but I can't say I was quite at believing him yet. All in all a really good story with beautiful depth. Safety: No Om/OW/Sharing while they are together. Others during their separation for one of them. No rape or abuse. </span>
  <a data-text-id="7714863451936773402" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText647824379975521768" style="display:none">I love this book! Simple as that. I am extremely happy that i got this ARC, because it was truly worth it and also i have a feeling this one will be a big hit.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1417040204ra/12181531.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The writing was stunning, the characters were insane but of the good kind and i adore them, i saw the many artful brushes here and there that connected the past with the present and the character development was a serious plus. Also the sentiments that the story ignited in my heart, were explosive.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1417039664ra/12181292.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My heart was jumping around my chest all the time, this book which is filled with chemistry angst and feelings was exactly what i needed. In the end i kept trying to flip onto the next page, but there was none, so now i have to wait and pray for the next book to be out.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395755912ra/9040230.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ethan broke Cassie's heart! Completely, he shattered her, he changed her, put her back together and eventually he left. But now he is back and Cassie, has no idea of how to forgive him. Is he really the changed person he claims to be? Can she ever trust him again? For the third time? How bad or dark, could this Romeo, really be?<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1417039664ra/12181291.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ethan Holt, with the amazing name and the gorgeous face, is also a crazily disturbed, rugged, unbelievably talented, sexy as hell difficult person, who tries his best to avoid his real feelings, but that wasn't one bit the cliche that comes straight in mind = bad boy + intimacy issues. His personality is entirely superb and unique.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417039664i/12181293.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Cassie Taylor, also beautiful, starts as a people pleaser, but changes her ways quickly and takes a leap of faith in herself, when she decides to become an actress. She is trustworthy, talented, romantic, but also vivacious and sometimes cynical. Her relationship with Ethan, will shape her into a closed off person with trust issues.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417039664i/12181294._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>No matter what i write, i feel that i can do no justice to this book. Thank you.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1417040204ra/12181532.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>THOUGHTS ABOUT THE BOOK<br><br>- I seriously LOVED IT! Because when it finally happened. Wow! <br>- The way it is writen with all the past and present unravelling simultaneously was extraordinary and well-handled.<br><br><br><i>ARC provided via Netgalley in exchange of an honest review. <div id="review_1259920809" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1259920809" />
    <a title="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover"><img alt="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1489089790p2/34338862.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1259920809?book_show_action=true">Apr 20, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" class="user" itemprop="url" name="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" href="/user/show/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover">TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1259920809" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11485527494287182130"><b>I loved it I loved it I loved it (1,162 times)</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429730293i/14625107._SY540_.jpg' width='350' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>What a debut! I honestly was blown away that this was Leisa Rayven’s first book and I kind of want to kick myself for waiting so long to read this. I haven’t read a story like this in quite some time. And in all honesty, it made me appreciate words that were written so insanely well, that I had a smile on my face the whole time I was reading. <br/><br/>Sometimes I think we can get lost and caught up in lust and romance and sexual fluff in books (and hey- I am</span>
  <span id="freeText11485527494287182130" style="display:none"><b>I loved it I loved it I loved it (1,162 times)</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429730293i/14625107._SY540_.jpg" width="350" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>What a debut! I honestly was blown away that this was Leisa Rayven’s first book and I kind of want to kick myself for waiting so long to read this. I haven’t read a story like this in quite some time. And in all honesty, it made me appreciate words that were written so insanely well, that I had a smile on my face the whole time I was reading. <br><br>Sometimes I think we can get lost and caught up in lust and romance and sexual fluff in books (and hey- I am guilty as charged) and forget what a damn well written book actually looks like. Well, this right here is it. If you’re looking for a steamy read with an alpha male that is full of sex scenes, this is not it. Instead, what you’ll get is a phenomenally written story (I can’t stress her amazing writing enough) about two broken flawed people just trying to get through college and then eventually heartbreak.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Everything I’ve ever known is now rewritten by my need for him.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429730293i/14625108._SY540_.jpg" width="350" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I can totally see why some reviews on here weren’t so favorable. Why Cassie could come across as annoying and why Ethan seemed like a total asshole. Well, in my opinion, it’s because they were. But I think when you strip away their flaws and you just look at the story in front of you, a story about a girl so consumed with love she loses herself and a boy so insecure he lashes out on others and makes stupid mistakes, you get something SO REAL.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429730293i/14625109._SY540_.jpg" width="350" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“I’m going to ruin you for all other women,” I say seriously. He nods. “Too late.”</i>
</b><br><br>I would pay anyone a pretty penny to show me a girl at that age that hasn’t at one point been completely blinded by her attraction to someone that it turns her into a raging hormonal lunatic (again, guilty as charged. I can without shame say when I was her age, boys took over my thoughts constantly). As for Ethan? Yea, he pretty much reminded me of every little twit I was infatuated with at their age. Rude, up and down, indecisive. Leisa hit the nail right on the head!<br><br><b>
  <i>”Love is weakness. That’s not the only thing he taught me, but it’s the thing I remember most.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429730293i/14625110._SY540_.jpg" width="350" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But again, when you look beyond all that, Bad Romeo was a beautifully written story, with such angst and sexual tension I thought my head was going to explode. It was a HYSTERICAL (I need to stress that, too), sweet, sad, romantic, and exciting read all wrapped into one nice little package. I thought the characters were real and raw and amazing, and I cannot wait until Broken Juliet comes out!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429730293i/14625111._SY540_.jpg" width="350" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="11485527494287182130" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stephanie • Ideally Inspired" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stephanie • Ideally Inspired" href="/user/show/8422973-stephanie-ideally-inspired">Stephanie • Ideally Inspired</a>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422973-stephanie-ideally-inspired?shelf=ain-t-nobody-got-time-for-that">ain-t-nobody-got-time-for-that</a>,

          </div>
