        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1087645136" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7157154137717856932">NOPE. NO. ABSOLUTELY NOT. <br/><br/>Review coming...unlike Ethan.<br/><br/><a href='http://nobsbookreviews.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/DNF.jpg' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411603090i/11254397._SX540_.jpg' alt='DNF' width='789' height='317' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/> <br/> 
  <strong>
    <em>"O Romeo, Romeo, wherefore art thou Romeo?" </em>
  </strong>
 <br/>Hope you're not looking for him here, cause HE AIN'T IN THIS BOOK.<br/><br/>Don't worry though, I wasn't expecting to find him in this book either.<br/><br/>Before I get into my review, I want to point out that this book has been getting a lot of buzz around the blogosphere. A lot of people are picking up what this author is putting down. I however, am not drinking the Kool-Aid.<br/><br/>I decided to give thi</span>
  <span id="freeText7157154137717856932" style="display:none">NOPE. NO. ABSOLUTELY NOT. <br><br>Review coming...unlike Ethan.<br><br><a href="http://nobsbookreviews.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/DNF.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411603090i/11254397._SX540_.jpg" alt="DNF" width="789" height="317" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br> <br> 
  <strong>
    <em>"O Romeo, Romeo, wherefore art thou Romeo?" </em>
  </strong>
 <br>Hope you're not looking for him here, cause HE AIN'T IN THIS BOOK.<br><br>Don't worry though, I wasn't expecting to find him in this book either.<br><br>Before I get into my review, I want to point out that this book has been getting a lot of buzz around the blogosphere. A lot of people are picking up what this author is putting down. I however, am not drinking the Kool-Aid.<br><br>I decided to give this book a try after several of my blogging buddies gushed over how incredible this book was. How amazing the sexual tension is. How this is one of the best books they've EVER READ within this genre.<br><br>So I picked it up.<br><br>I was ready for the awesome.<br><br>I was excited to be blown away.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1414505109ra/11660807.gif" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But guess what?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405364067ra/10386916.gif" alt="frustrated animated GIF " width="576" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Instead of being amazed, I was left frustrated &amp; annoyed.<img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385866274ra/7246697.gif" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book was like a broken record, that was replaying the same busted track that you can't seem to get out of your head. <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1404306060ra/10222781.gif" alt="" width="358" height="233" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For the first 15-20%, I won't lie, the author had me invested in the story. There was humor, and nice, healthy, sexual tension.<br><br>But then, beyond 20% shit just got to be: <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415252122i/11757764.gif" alt="" width="455" height="200" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415252122ra/11757765.gif" alt="" width="682" height="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story is so incredibly underwhelming. The characters felt one-dimensional.<br><br>The hero, Ethan Holt: ASSHOLE.<br><br>The heroine Cassie Taylor: DELUSIONAL.<br><br>At 50%, I had to put my Kindle down and phone (well Facebook IM) a friend:<br><br><a href="http://nobsbookreviews.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/Screen-Shot-2014-11-05-at-11.14.25-PM.png" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415252122ra/11757766.gif" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://nobsbookreviews.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/Screen-Shot-2014-11-05-at-11.14.25-PM.png" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415252122i/11757767.png" alt="Screen Shot 2014-11-05 at 11.14.25 PM" width="464" height="433" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415252122i/11757768.jpg" alt="Screen Shot 2014-11-05 at 11.14.47 PM" width="460" height="376" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You'd think I would've just DNF'd at 50%, and just called it a day. BUT NO, I subjected myself to another 20% (DNF'd at 71%) only to wish I could lobotomize myself.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415252122ra/11757769.gif" alt="" width="500" height="388" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If I could summarize this book in 5 words: BLUE BALLS AND DRY HUMPS. <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415252122ra/11757770.gif" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To me, this book was a literal interpretation of Lady Gaga's song: Bad Romance.<br><br>No matter how many times Ethan told Cassie that he was bad for her, she still aggressively pursued him. <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415252122ra/11757771.gif" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>WHERE IS YOUR SELF RESPECT?<br><br>Girl, you cray.<img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412966098ra/11449136.gif" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>By 70%, I. Couldn't. Care. Less.<br><br>I have a message to the couple in this story:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415252122ra/11757772.gif" alt="" width="574" height="240" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Or wait, I guess you can't, cause this book was the biggest cock tease I've ever read.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412434841ra/11375219.gif" alt="" width="504" height="264" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> </span>
  <a data-text-id="7157154137717856932" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('AH1uVHJ+zhlAUjqwsRDtYBx3MrDvDmvk9GNyhqC/F1KIMorpHeJrPmXLJ0z+oXAkNdXvPaQoeUj05+HFkR1XFw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('+/UpXB19Vl/ULlTshyf+r4u9b9PQ2xCa6nTL45oBLuBzus3hcuHzePG3SRDIlmProh+yXpv9Ajbq8Figq6NupQ==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

      var newTip = new Tip($('bookCover_25564665'), "\n\n  <h2><a class=\"readable bookTitle\" href=\"https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25564665-the-mistake?from_choice=false&amp;from_home_module=false\">The Mistake (Off-Campus, #2)<\/a><\/h2>\n\n      <div>\n        by <a class=\"authorName\" href=\"/author/show/1935000.Elle_Kennedy?a=9&amp;origin=related_works\">Elle Kennedy<\/a><span title=\"Goodreads Author!\">*<\/span>\n      <\/div>\n\n          <div class=\"smallText uitext darkGreyText\">\n            <span class=\"minirating\"><span class=\"stars staticStars notranslate\"><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p3\"><\/span><\/span> 4.12 avg rating &mdash; 71,254 ratings<\/span>            &mdash; published 2015\n          <\/div>\n\n    <div class=\"addBookTipDescription\">\n      \n<span id=\"freeTextContainer16062872577984307480\">He’s a player in more ways than one…\n\nCollege junior John Logan can get any girl he wants. For this hockey star, life is a parade of parties and hook-ups, but behind his killer grins and easygoing charm, he hides growing despair about the dead-end ro<\/span>\n  <span id=\"freeText16062872577984307480\" style=\"display:none\">He’s a player in more ways than one…\n\nCollege junior John Logan can get any girl he wants. For this hockey star, life is a parade of parties and hook-ups, but behind his killer grins and easygoing charm, he hides growing despair about the dead-end road he’ll be forced to walk after graduation.
